class="mt-4 grid items-start gap-10 lg:grid-cols-[minmax(0,1fr)_auto]" data-testid="templates/details/content"><div class="order-2 lg:order-1"><div class="space-y-4 whitespace-normal min-w-0 [&amp;&gt;*:first-child]:mt-0 [&amp;&gt;*:last-child]:mb-0"><h2 class="mt-8 mb-4 text-[32px] leading-10 font-semibold tracking-[-0.79px]">Slack Agent Template</h2>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900"><a href="https://vercel.com/new/clone?demo-description=This%20is%20a%20Slack%20Agent%20template%20built%20with%20Bolt%20for%20JavaScript%20(TypeScript)%20and%20the%20Nitro%20server%20framework.&amp;demo-image=%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fe5382hct74si%2FSs9t7RkKlPtProrbDhZFM%2F0d11b9095ecf84c87a68fbdef6f12ad1%2FFrame__1_.png&amp;demo-title=Slack%20Agent%20Template&amp;demo-url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fvercel-partner-solutions%2Fslack-agent-template&amp;env=SLACK_SIGNING_SECRET%2CSLACK_BOT_TOKEN&amp;envDescription=These%20environment%20variables%20are%20required%20to%20deploy%20your%20Slack%20app%20to%20Vercel&amp;envLink=https%3A%2F%2Fapi.slack.com%2Fapps&amp;from=templates&amp;project-name=Slack%20Agent%20Template&amp;project-names=Comma%20separated%20list%20of%20project%20names%2Cto%20match%20the%20root-directories&amp;repository-name=slack-agent-template&amp;repository-url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fvercel-partner-solutions%2Fslack-agent-template&amp;root-directories=List%20of%20directory%20paths%20for%20the%20directories%20to%20clone%20into%20projects&amp;skippable-integrations=1" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"></a></p>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">A Slack Agent template built with <a href="https://useworkflow.dev/" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">Workflow DevKit</a>&#x27;s <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">DurableAgent</code>, <a href="https://ai-sdk.dev/" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">AI SDK</a> tools, <a href="https://tools.slack.dev/bolt-js/" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">Bolt for JavaScript</a> (TypeScript), and the <a href="https://nitro.build/" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">Nitro</a> server framework.</p>
<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">Features</h3>
<ul class="list-module__7sPsqG__ul">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong"><a href="https://useworkflow.dev/" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">Workflow DevKit</a></span> — Make any TypeScript function durable. Build AI agents that can suspend, resume, and maintain state with ease. Reliability-as-code with automatic retries and observability built in</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong"><a href="https://ai-sdk.dev/" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">AI SDK</a></span> — The AI Toolkit for TypeScript. Define type-safe tools with schema validation and switch between AI providers by changing a single line of code</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong"><a href="https://vercel.com/ai-gateway" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">Vercel AI Gateway</a></span> — One endpoint, all your models. Access hundreds of AI models through a centralized interface with intelligent failovers and no rate limits</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong"><a href="https://api.slack.com/docs/apps/ai" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">Slack Assistant</a></span> — Integrates with Slack&#x27;s Assistant API for threaded conversations with real-time streaming responses</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/lib/ai/workflows/hooks.ts" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">Human-in-the-Loop</a></span> — Built-in approval workflows that pause agent execution until a user approves sensitive actions like joining channels</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/lib/ai/tools.ts" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">Built-in Tools</a></span> — Pre-configured tools for reading channels, threads, joining channels (with approval), and searching</li>
</ul>
<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">Prerequisites</h3>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">Before getting started, make sure you have a development workspace where you have permissions to install apps. You can use a <a href="https://api.slack.com/developer-program" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">developer sandbox</a> or <a href="https://slack.com/create" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">create a workspace</a>.</p>
<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">Getting Started</h3>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4">Clone and install dependencies</h4>

<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4">Create a Slack App</h4>
<ol class="list-module__7sPsqG__ol">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Open <a href="https://api.slack.com/apps/new" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">https://api.slack.com/apps/new</a> and choose &quot;From an app manifest&quot;</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Choose the workspace you want to use</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Copy the contents of <a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/manifest.json" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">manifest.json</code></a> into the text box that says &quot;Paste your manifest code here&quot; (JSON tab) and click Next</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Review the configuration and click Create</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">On the Install App tab, click Install to &lt;Workspace_Name&gt;
<ul class="list-module__7sPsqG__ul">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">You will be redirected to the App Configuration dashboard</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Copy the Bot User OAuth Token into your environment as <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">SLACK_BOT_TOKEN</code></li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">On the Basic Information tab, copy your Signing Secret into your environment as <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">SLACK_SIGNING_SECRET</code></li>
</ol>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4">Environment Setup</h4>
<ol class="list-module__7sPsqG__ol">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Add your <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">AI_GATEWAY_API_KEY</code> to your <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">.env</code> file. You can get one <a href="https://vercel.com/d?to=%2F%5Bteam%5D%2F%7E%2Fai%2Fapi-keys%3Futm_source%3Dai_gateway_landing_page&amp;title=Get+an+API+Key" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">here</a></li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Add your <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">NGROK_AUTH_TOKEN</code> to your <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">.env</code> file. You can get one <a href="https://dashboard.ngrok.com/login?state=X1FFBj9sgtS9-oFK_2-h15Xcg0zHPjp_b9edWYrpGBVvIluUPEAarKRIjpp8ZeCHNTljTyreeslpG6n8anuSCFUkgIxwLypEGOa4Ci_cmnXYLhOfYogHWB6TzWBYUmhFLPW0XeGn789mFV_muomVd7QizkgwuYW8Vz2wW315YIK5UPywQaIGFKV8" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">here</a></li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">In the terminal run <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">slack app link</code></li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">If prompted <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">update the manifest source to remote</code> select <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">yes</code></li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Copy your App ID from the app you just created</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Select <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">Local</code> when prompted</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Open <a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/.slack/config.json" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">.slack/config.json</code></a> and update your manifest source to <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">local</code></li>
</ol>
<pre><div class="relative rounded-md border border-[var(--ds-gray-400)] overflow-hidden group/copy my-4 h-auto language-json" data-geist-code-block=""><button type="button" tabindex="0" class="code-block-module__vF3MAa__lineNumber">6</button><div class="token-line"><span class="token plain"></span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></div></div></code></pre></div></pre>
<ol class="list-module__7sPsqG__ol">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Start your local server using <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">slack run</code>. If prompted, select the workspace you&#x27;d like to grant access to
<ul class="list-module__7sPsqG__ul">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Select <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">yes</code> if asked &quot;Update app settings with changes to the local manifest?&quot;</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Open your Slack workspace and add your new Slack Agent to a channel. Your Slack Agent should respond whenever it&#x27;s tagged in a message or sent a DM</li>
</ol>
<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">Deploy to Vercel</h3>
<ol class="list-module__7sPsqG__ol">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Create a new Slack app for production following the steps from above</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Create a new Vercel project <a href="https://vercel.com/new" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">here</a> and select this repo</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Copy the Bot User OAuth Token into your Vercel environment variables as <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">SLACK_BOT_TOKEN</code></li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">On the Basic Information tab, copy your Signing Secret into your Vercel environment variables as <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">SLACK_SIGNING_SECRET</code></li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">When your deployment has finished, open your App Manifest from the Slack App Dashboard</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Update the manifest so all the <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">request_url</code> and <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">url</code> fields use <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">https://&lt;your-app-domain&gt;/api/slack/events</code></li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Click save and you will be prompted to verify the URL</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Open your Slack workspace and add your new Slack Agent to a channel. Your Slack Agent should respond whenever it&#x27;s tagged in a message or sent a DM
<ul class="list-module__7sPsqG__ul">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><em>Note</em>: Make sure you add the production app, not the local app we setup earlier</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Your app will now automatically build and deploy whenever you commit to your repo. More information <a href="https://vercel.com/docs/git" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">here</a></li>
</ol>
<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">Project Structure</h3>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/manifest.json" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">manifest.json</code></a></h4>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/manifest.json" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">manifest.json</code></a> is a configuration for Slack apps. With a manifest, you can create an app with a pre-defined configuration, or adjust the configuration of an existing app.</p>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/app.ts" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/app.ts</code></a></h4>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/app.ts" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/app.ts</code></a> is the entry point of the application. This file is kept minimal and primarily serves to route inbound requests.</p>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/lib/ai" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/lib/ai</code></a></h4>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">Contains the AI agent implementation:</p>
<ul class="list-module__7sPsqG__ul">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/lib/ai/agent.ts" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">agent.ts</code></a></span> — Creates the <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">DurableAgent</code> from Workflow with system instructions and available tools. The agent automatically handles tool calling loops until it has enough context to respond.</p>
</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/lib/ai/tools.ts" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">tools.ts</code></a></span> — Tool definitions using AI SDK&#x27;s <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">tool</code> function:</p>
<ul class="list-module__7sPsqG__ul">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">getChannelMessages</code> — Fetches recent messages from a Slack channel</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">getThreadMessages</code> — Fetches messages from a specific thread</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">joinChannel</code> — Joins a public Slack channel (with Human-in-the-Loop approval)</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">searchChannels</code> — Searches for channels by name, topic, or purpose</li>
</ul>
</li>
</ul>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/listeners" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/listeners</code></a></h4>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">Every incoming request is routed to a &quot;listener&quot;. Inside this directory, we group each listener based on the Slack Platform feature used:</p>
<ul class="list-module__7sPsqG__ul">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/listeners/assistant" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/listeners/assistant</code></a> — Handles Slack Assistant events (thread started, user message, context changed)</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/listeners/actions" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/listeners/actions</code></a> — Handles interactive component actions (buttons, menus) including HITL approval handlers</li>

<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/api" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/api</code></a></h4>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">This is your Nitro server API directory. Contains <a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/api/slack/events.post.ts" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">events.post.ts</code></a> which matches the request URL defined in your <a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/manifest.json" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">manifest.json</code></a>. Nitro uses file-based routing for incoming requests. Learn more <a href="https://nitro.build/guide/routing" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">here</a>.</p>
<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">Agent Architecture</h3>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4">Chat Workflow</h4>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">The core agent loop is implemented as a durable workflow using Workflow DevKit. When a user sends a message, the workflow orchestrates the agent&#x27;s response with automatic retry handling and streaming support.</p>

<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Key files:</span></p>
<ul class="list-module__7sPsqG__ul">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/lib/ai/workflows/chat.ts" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/lib/ai/workflows/chat.ts</code></a> — The durable workflow definition using <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">&quot;use workflow&quot;</code> directive</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/lib/ai/agent.ts" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/lib/ai/agent.ts</code></a> — Creates the <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">DurableAgent</code> with system prompt and tools</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/listeners/assistant/assistantUserMessage.ts" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/listeners/assistant/assistantUserMessage.ts</code></a> — Listener that starts the workflow and streams responses</li>
</ul>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">How it works:</span></p>
<ol class="list-module__7sPsqG__ol">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">User sends a message to the Slack Assistant</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">The <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">assistantUserMessage</code> listener collects thread context and starts the workflow</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">chatWorkflow</code> creates the agent and calls <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">agent.stream()</code> with the messages</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">The agent processes the request, calling tools as needed (each tool uses <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">&quot;use step&quot;</code> for durability)</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Response chunks are streamed back to Slack in real-time via <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">chatStream()</code></li>
</ol>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4">Human-in-the-Loop (HITL) Workflow</h4>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">This template demonstrates a production-ready Human-in-the-Loop pattern using Workflow DevKit&#x27;s <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">defineHook</code> primitive. When the agent needs to perform sensitive actions (like joining a channel), it pauses execution and waits for user approval.</p>

<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">Key files:</span></p>
<ul class="list-module__7sPsqG__ul">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/lib/ai/workflows/hooks.ts" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/lib/ai/workflows/hooks.ts</code></a> — Hook definitions for HITL workflows (e.g., <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">channelJoinApprovalHook</code>)</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/lib/ai/tools.ts" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/lib/ai/tools.ts</code></a> — Tool definitions including <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">joinChannel</code> which uses the approval hook</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/lib/slack/blocks.ts" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/lib/slack/blocks.ts</code></a> — Slack Block Kit UI for approval buttons</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/listeners/actions/channel-join-approval.ts" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/listeners/actions/channel-join-approval.ts</code></a> — Action handler that resumes the workflow</li>
</ul>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900"><span class="font-semibold" data-streamdown="strong">How it works:</span></p>
<ol class="list-module__7sPsqG__ol">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">The <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">joinChannel</code> tool is called by the agent</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">A Slack message with Approve/Reject buttons is posted to the thread</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">channelJoinApprovalHook.create()</code> creates a hook instance and the workflow pauses at <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">await hook</code></li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">When the user clicks a button, the action handler calls <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">hook.resume()</code> with the decision</li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">The workflow resumes and the agent either joins the channel or acknowledges the rejection</li>
</ol>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">This pattern can be extended for any action requiring human approval (e.g., sending messages, modifying data, external API calls).</p>
<h3 class="text-copy-24 mt-8 mb-4">Customizing the Agent</h3>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4">Modifying Instructions</h4>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">Edit the <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">system</code> prompt in <a href="https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template/tree/main/server/lib/ai/agent.ts" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline"><code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/lib/ai/agent.ts</code></a> to change how your agent behaves, responds, and uses tools.</p>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4">Adding New Tools</h4>
<ol class="list-module__7sPsqG__ol">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Add a new tool definition in <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/lib/ai/tools.ts</code> using AI SDK&#x27;s <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">tool</code> function:</li>
</ol>

<ol class="list-module__7sPsqG__ol">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Add it to the <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">slackTools</code> export in <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/lib/ai/tools.ts</code></li>
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Update the agent instructions in <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/lib/ai/agent.ts</code> to describe when to use the new tool</li>
</ol>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">Learn more about building agents with the AI SDK in the <a href="https://ai-sdk.dev/docs/agents" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">Agents documentation</a>.</p>
<h4 class="text-copy-20 mt-8 mb-4">Adding Human-in-the-Loop to Tools</h4>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">To add approval workflows to your own tools:</p>
<ol class="list-module__7sPsqG__ol">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Add a hook definition to <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">/server/lib/ai/workflows/hooks.ts</code>:</li>
</ol>

<ol class="list-module__7sPsqG__ol">
<li class="mb-2.5 text-[1em] leading-relaxed text-(--accents-5)">Create an action handler that calls <code class="text-[var(--geist-code)] font-mono whitespace-pre-wrap break-words py-px px-0.5 -my-px rounded-[4px] bg-[var(--accents-1)] border border-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:bg-[var(--accents-2)] dark-theme:border-[var(--accents-3)] text-copy-14">hook.resume()</code> when the user responds</li>
</ol>
<p class="text-copy-16 mx-4 text-gray-900">Learn more about hooks in the <a href="https://useworkflow.dev/docs/foundations/hooks" rel="nofollow noopener noreferrer" target="_blank" node="[object Object]" data-zone="null" class="link-module__Q1NRQq__link no-underline cursor-pointer text-blue-900 no-underline visited:text-blue-900 hover:text-blue-900 hover:no-underline">Workflow DevKit documentation</a>.</p>

Vercel](https://vercel.com/button)](\u003chttps://vercel.com/new/clone?demo-description=This%20is%20a%20Slack%20Agent%20template%20built%20with%20Bolt%20for%20JavaScript%20(TypeScript)%20and%20the%20Nitro%20server%20framework.\u0026demo-image=%2F%2Fimages.ctfassets.net%2Fe5382hct74si%2FSs9t7RkKlPtProrbDhZFM%2F0d11b9095ecf84c87a68fbdef6f12ad1%2FFrame__1_.png\u0026demo-title=Slack%20Agent%20Template\u0026demo-url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fvercel-partner-solutions%2Fslack-agent-template\u0026env=SLACK_SIGNING_SECRET%2CSLACK_BOT_TOKEN\u0026envDescription=These%20environment%20variables%20are%20required%20to%20deploy%20your%20Slack%20app%20to%20Vercel\u0026envLink=https%3A%2F%2Fapi.slack.com%2Fapps\u0026from=templates\u0026project-name=Slack%20Agent%20Template\u0026project-names=Comma%20separated%20list%20of%20project%20names%2Cto%20match%20the%20root-directories\u0026repository-name=slack-agent-template\u0026repository-url=https%3A%2F%2Fgithub.com%2Fvercel-partner-solutions%2Fslack-agent-template\u0026root-directories=List%20of%20directory%20paths%20for%20the%20directories%20to%20clone%20into%20projects\u0026skippable-integrations=1\u003e)\n\nA Slack Agent template built with [Workflow DevKit](https://useworkflow.dev)'s `DurableAgent`, [AI SDK](https://ai-sdk.dev) tools, [Bolt for JavaScript](https://tools.slack.dev/bolt-js/) (TypeScript), and the [Nitro](https://nitro.build) server framework.\n\n## Features\n\n- **[Workflow DevKit](https://useworkflow.dev)** — Make any TypeScript function durable. Build AI agents that can suspend, resume, and maintain state with ease. Reliability-as-code with automatic retries and observability built in\n- **[AI SDK](https://ai-sdk.dev)** — The AI Toolkit for TypeScript. Define type-safe tools with schema validation and switch between AI providers by changing a single line of code\n- **[Vercel AI Gateway](https://vercel.com/ai-gateway)** — One endpoint, all your models. Access hundreds of AI models through a centralized interface with intelligent failovers and no rate limits\n- **[Slack Assistant](https://api.slack.com/docs/apps/ai)** — Integrates with Slack's Assistant API for threaded conversations with real-time streaming responses\n- **[Human-in-the-Loop](./server/lib/ai/workflows/hooks.ts)** — Built-in approval workflows that pause agent execution until a user approves sensitive actions like joining channels\n- **[Built-in Tools](./server/lib/ai/tools.ts)** — Pre-configured tools for reading channels, threads, joining channels (with approval), and searching\n\n## Prerequisites\n\nBefore getting started, make sure you have a development workspace where you have permissions to install apps. You can use a [developer sandbox](https://api.slack.com/developer-program) or [create a workspace](https://slack.com/create).\n\n## Getting Started\n\n### Clone and install dependencies\n\n```bash\ngit clone https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template \u0026\u0026 cd slack-agent-template \u0026\u0026 pnpm install\n```\n\n### Create a Slack App\n\n1. Open https://api.slack.com/apps/new and choose \"From an app manifest\"\n2. Choose the workspace you want to use\n3. Copy the contents of [`manifest.json`](./manifest.json) into the text box that says \"Paste your manifest code here\" (JSON tab) and click Next\n4. Review the configuration and click Create\n5. On the Install App tab, click Install to \u003cWorkspace_Name\u003e\n   - You will be redirected to the App Configuration dashboard\n6. Copy the Bot User OAuth Token into your environment as `SLACK_BOT_TOKEN`\n7. On the Basic Information tab, copy your Signing Secret into your environment as `SLACK_SIGNING_SECRET`\n\n### Environment Setup\n\n1. Add your `AI_GATEWAY_API_KEY` to your `.env` file. You can get one [here](https://vercel.com/d?to=%2F%5Bteam%5D%2F%7E%2Fai%2Fapi-keys%3Futm_source%3Dai_gateway_landing_page\u0026title=Get+an+API+Key)\n2. Add your `NGROK_AUTH_TOKEN` to your `.env` file. You can get one [here](https://dashboard.ngrok.com/login?state=X1FFBj9sgtS9-oFK_2-h15Xcg0zHPjp_b9edWYrpGBVvIluUPEAarKRIjpp8ZeCHNTljTyreeslpG6n8anuSCFUkgIxwLypEGOa4Ci_cmnXYLhOfYogHWB6TzWBYUmhFLPW0XeGn789mFV_muomVd7QizkgwuYW8Vz2wW315YIK5UPywQaIGFKV8)\n3. In the terminal run `slack app link`\n4. If prompted `update the manifest source to remote` select `yes`\n5. Copy your App ID from the app you just created\n6. Select `Local` when prompted\n7. Open [`.slack/config.json`](./.slack/config.json) and update your manifest source to `local`\n\n```json\n{\n  \"manifest\": {\n    \"source\": \"local\"\n  },\n  \"project_id\": \"\u003cproject-id-added-by-slack-cli\u003e\"\n}\n```\n\n8. Start your local server using `slack run`. If prompted, select the workspace you'd like to grant access to\n   - Select `yes` if asked \"Update app settings with changes to the local manifest?\"\n9. Open your Slack workspace and add your new Slack Agent to a channel. Your Slack Agent should respond whenever it's tagged in a message or sent a DM\n\n## Deploy to Vercel\n\n1. Create a new Slack app for production following the steps from above\n2. Create a new Vercel project [here](https://vercel.com/new) and select this repo\n3. Copy the Bot User OAuth Token into your Vercel environment variables as `SLACK_BOT_TOKEN`\n4. On the Basic Information tab, copy your Signing Secret into your Vercel environment variables as `SLACK_SIGNING_SECRET`\n5. When your deployment has finished, open your App Manifest from the Slack App Dashboard\n6. Update the manifest so all the `request_url` and `url` fields use `https://\u003cyour-app-domain\u003e/api/slack/events`\n7. Click save and you will be prompted to verify the URL\n8. Open your Slack workspace and add your new Slack Agent to a channel. Your Slack Agent should respond whenever it's tagged in a message or sent a DM\n   - _Note_: Make sure you add the production app, not the local app we setup earlier\n9. Your app will now automatically build and deploy whenever you commit to your repo. More information [here](https://vercel.com/docs/git)\n\n## Project Structure\n\n### [`manifest.json`](./manifest.json)\n\n[`manifest.json`](./manifest.json) is a configuration for Slack apps. With a manifest, you can create an app with a pre-defined configuration, or adjust the configuration of an existing app.\n\n### [`/server/app.ts`](./server/app.ts)\n\n[`/server/app.ts`](./server/app.ts) is the entry point of the application. This file is kept minimal and primarily serves to route inbound requests.\n\n### [`/server/lib/ai`](./server/lib/ai)\n\nContains the AI agent implementation:\n\n- **[`agent.ts`](./server/lib/ai/agent.ts)** — Creates the `DurableAgent` from Workflow with system instructions and available tools. The agent automatically handles tool calling loops until it has enough context to respond.\n\n- **[`tools.ts`](./server/lib/ai/tools.ts)** — Tool definitions using AI SDK's `tool` function:\n  - `getChannelMessages` — Fetches recent messages from a Slack channel\n  - `getThreadMessages` — Fetches messages from a specific thread\n  - `joinChannel` — Joins a public Slack channel (with Human-in-the-Loop approval)\n  - `searchChannels` — Searches for channels by name, topic, or purpose\n\n### [`/server/listeners`](./server/listeners)\n\nEvery incoming request is routed to a \"listener\". Inside this directory, we group each listener based on the Slack Platform feature used:\n\n- [`/listeners/assistant`](./server/listeners/assistant) — Handles Slack Assistant events (thread started, user message, context changed)\n- [`/listeners/actions`](./server/listeners/actions) — Handles interactive component actions (buttons, menus) including HITL approval handlers\n- [`/listeners/shortcuts`](./server/listeners/shortcuts/index.ts) — Handles incoming [Shortcuts](https://api.slack.com/interactivity/shortcuts) requests\n- [`/listeners/views`](./server/listeners/views/index.ts) — Handles [View submissions](https://api.slack.com/reference/interaction-payloads/views#view_submission)\n- [`/listeners/events`](./server/listeners/events) — Handles Slack events like app mentions and home tab opens\n\n### [`/server/api`](./server/api)\n\nThis is your Nitro server API directory. Contains [`events.post.ts`](./server/api/slack/events.post.ts) which matches the request URL defined in your [`manifest.json`](./manifest.json). Nitro uses file-based routing for incoming requests. Learn more [here](https://nitro.build/guide/routing).\n\n## Agent Architecture\n\n### Chat Workflow\n\nThe core agent loop is implemented as a durable workflow using Workflow DevKit. When a user sends a message, the workflow orchestrates the agent's response with automatic retry handling and streaming support.\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                       Chat Workflow                             │\n├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤\n│                                                                 │\n│  User Message ──▶ assistantUserMessage listener                 │\n│                              │                                  │\n│                              ▼                                  │\n│                   ┌─────────────────────┐                       │\n│                   │  start(chatWorkflow)│                       │\n│                   │  with messages +    │                       │\n│                   │  context            │                       │\n│                   └─────────────────────┘                       │\n│                              │                                  │\n│                              ▼                                  │\n│                   ┌─────────────────────┐                       │\n│                   │  createSlackAgent() │                       │\n│                   │  with tools         │                       │\n│                   └─────────────────────┘                       │\n│                              │                                  │\n│                              ▼                                  │\n│                   ┌─────────────────────┐                       │\n│                   │  agent.stream()     │──▶ Tool calls         │\n│                   │  generates response │    (may loop)         │\n│                   └─────────────────────┘                       │\n│                              │                                  │\n│                              ▼                                  │\n│                   ┌─────────────────────┐                       │\n│                   │  Stream chunks to   │                       │\n│                   │  Slack via          │                       │\n│                   │  chatStream()       │                       │\n│                   └─────────────────────┘                       │\n│                              │                                  │\n│                              ▼                                  │\n│                        User sees response                       │\n│                                                                 │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n**Key files:**\n\n- [`/server/lib/ai/workflows/chat.ts`](./server/lib/ai/workflows/chat.ts) — The durable workflow definition using `\"use workflow\"` directive\n- [`/server/lib/ai/agent.ts`](./server/lib/ai/agent.ts) — Creates the `DurableAgent` with system prompt and tools\n- [`/server/listeners/assistant/assistantUserMessage.ts`](./server/listeners/assistant/assistantUserMessage.ts) — Listener that starts the workflow and streams responses\n\n**How it works:**\n\n1. User sends a message to the Slack Assistant\n2. The `assistantUserMessage` listener collects thread context and starts the workflow\n3. `chatWorkflow` creates the agent and calls `agent.stream()` with the messages\n4. The agent processes the request, calling tools as needed (each tool uses `\"use step\"` for durability)\n5. Response chunks are streamed back to Slack in real-time via `chatStream()`\n\n### Human-in-the-Loop (HITL) Workflow\n\nThis template demonstrates a production-ready Human-in-the-Loop pattern using Workflow DevKit's `defineHook` primitive. When the agent needs to perform sensitive actions (like joining a channel), it pauses execution and waits for user approval.\n\n```\n┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐\n│                         HITL Flow                               │\n├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤\n│                                                                 │\n│  User Request ──▶ Agent ──▶ joinChannel Tool                    │\n│                                    │                            │\n│                                    ▼                            │\n│                        ┌─────────────────────┐                  │\n│                        │  Send Slack message │                  │\n│                        │  with Approve/Reject│                  │\n│                        │  buttons            │                  │\n│                        └─────────────────────┘                  │\n│                                    │                            │\n│                                    ▼                            │\n│                        ┌─────────────────────┐                  │\n│                        │  Workflow PAUSES    │                  │\n│                        │  (no compute used)  │◀── await hook    │\n│                        └─────────────────────┘                  │\n│                                    │                            │\n│                         User clicks button                      │\n│                                    │                            │\n│                                    ▼                            │\n│                        ┌─────────────────────┐                  │\n│                        │  Action handler     │                  │\n│                        │  calls hook.resume()│                  │\n│                        └─────────────────────┘                  │\n│                                    │                            │\n│                                    ▼                            │\n│                        ┌─────────────────────┐                  │\n│                        │  Workflow RESUMES   │                  │\n│                        │  with approval data │                  │\n│                        └─────────────────────┘                  │\n│                                    │                            │\n│                                    ▼                            │\n│                           Agent responds                        │\n│                                                                 │\n└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘\n```\n\n**Key files:**\n\n- [`/server/lib/ai/workflows/hooks.ts`](./server/lib/ai/workflows/hooks.ts) — Hook definitions for HITL workflows (e.g., `channelJoinApprovalHook`)\n- [`/server/lib/ai/tools.ts`](./server/lib/ai/tools.ts) — Tool definitions including `joinChannel` which uses the approval hook\n- [`/server/lib/slack/blocks.ts`](./server/lib/slack/blocks.ts) — Slack Block Kit UI for approval buttons\n- [`/server/listeners/actions/channel-join-approval.ts`](./server/listeners/actions/channel-join-approval.ts) — Action handler that resumes the workflow\n\n**How it works:**\n\n1. The `joinChannel` tool is called by the agent\n2. A Slack message with Approve/Reject buttons is posted to the thread\n3. `channelJoinApprovalHook.create()` creates a hook instance and the workflow pauses at `await hook`\n4. When the user clicks a button, the action handler calls `hook.resume()` with the decision\n5. The workflow resumes and the agent either joins the channel or acknowledges the rejection\n\nThis pattern can be extended for any action requiring human approval (e.g., sending messages, modifying data, external API calls).\n\n## Customizing the Agent\n\n### Modifying Instructions\n\nEdit the `system` prompt in [`/server/lib/ai/agent.ts`](./server/lib/ai/agent.ts) to change how your agent behaves, responds, and uses tools.\n\n### Adding New Tools\n\n1. Add a new tool definition in `/server/lib/ai/tools.ts` using AI SDK's `tool` function:\n\n```typescript\nimport { tool } from \"ai\";\nimport { z } from \"zod\";\nimport type { SlackAgentContextInput } from \"~/lib/ai/context\";\n\nconst myNewTool = tool({\n  description: \"Description of what this tool does\",\n  inputSchema: z.object({\n    param: z.string().describe(\"Parameter description\"),\n  }),\n  execute: async ({ param }, { experimental_context }) =\u003e {\n    \"use step\"; // Required for Workflow's durable execution\n\n    // Dynamic imports inside step to avoid bundling Node.js modules in workflow\n    const { WebClient } = await import(\"@slack/web-api\");\n\n    const ctx = experimental_context as SlackAgentContextInput;\n    const client = new WebClient(ctx.token);\n    // Tool implementation\n    return { result: \"...\" };\n  },\n});\n```\n\n2. Add it to the `slackTools` export in `/server/lib/ai/tools.ts`\n3. Update the agent instructions in `/server/lib/ai/agent.ts` to describe when to use the new tool\n\nLearn more about building agents with the AI SDK in the [Agents documentation](https://ai-sdk.dev/docs/agents).\n\n### Adding Human-in-the-Loop to Tools\n\nTo add approval workflows to your own tools:\n\n1. Add a hook definition to `/server/lib/ai/workflows/hooks.ts`:\n\n```typescript\nimport { defineHook } from \"workflow\";\nimport { z } from \"zod\";\n\nexport const myApprovalHook = defineHook({\n  schema: z.object({\n    approved: z.boolean(),\n    // Add any additional data you need\n  }),\n});\n```\n\n2. In your tool's execute function (without `\"use step\"`), create and await the hook:\n\n```typescript\nexecute: async ({ param }, { toolCallId, experimental_context }) =\u003e {\n  const ctx = experimental_context as SlackAgentContextInput;\n\n  // Send approval UI to user (in a step)\n  await sendApprovalMessage(ctx, toolCallId);\n\n  // Create hook and wait for approval (in workflow context)\n  const hook = myApprovalHook.create({ token: toolCallId });\n  const { approved } = await hook;\n\n  if (!approved) {\n    return { success: false, message: \"User declined\" };\n  }\n\n  // Perform the action (in a step)\n  return await performAction(ctx);\n};\n```\n\n3. Create an action handler that calls `hook.resume()` when the user responds\n\nLearn more about hooks in the [Workflow DevKit documentation](https://useworkflow.dev/docs/foundations/hooks).\n\n## Learn More\n\n- [Workflow DevKit Documentation](https://useworkflow.dev/docs)\n- [AI SDK Documentation](https://ai-sdk.dev)\n- [Slack Bolt Documentation](https://tools.slack.dev/bolt-js/)\n- [Slack Assistant API](https://api.slack.com/docs/apps/ai)\n- [Nitro Documentation](https://nitro.build)\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"40:[\"$\",\"$L4b\",null,{\"githubUrl\":\"https://github.com/vercel-partner-solutions/slack-agent-template\",\"readmeText\":\"$4c\"}]\n42:null\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"21:null\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"26:[[\"$\",\"title\",\"0\",{\"children\":\"Slack
